6/8/23, 08:47 - Saurabh Bhau College: # A Python closure is a function object that remembers values in the enclosing scope,
# even if they are not present in memory. It is a record that stores a function together
# with an environment, which is a mapping associating each free variable of the function
# (variables that are used locally but defined in an enclosing scope) with the value or
# reference to which the name was bound when the closure was created. In simpler terms,
# a closure is a function that has access to variables from its outer (enclosing) scope,
# even after the outer function has finished executing.
def output_decorator(operation):
    def decorator(func):
        def wrapper(x, y):
            result = func(x, y)
            print(f"Two number {operation} is {result}")
        return wrapper
    return decorator

@output_decorator("addition")
def addition(x, y):
    return x + y

@output_decorator("subtraction")
def subtraction(x, y):
    return x - y

@output_decorator("multiplication")
def multiplication(x, y):
    return x * y

addition(5, 3)
subtraction(7, 4)
multiplication(2, 6)

matrix = [[1, 2, 3], [4, 5, 6], [7, 8, 9]]
transposed_matrix = [list(row) for row in zip(*matrix)]
print(transposed_matrix)

#b)
days = ["Sunday", "Monday", "Tuesday", "Wednesday", "Thursday", "Friday", "Saturday"]
temp_C = [30.5, 32.6, 31.8, 33.4, 29.8, 30.2, 29.9]
weather_dict = {day: temperature for day, temperature in zip(days, temp_C)}
print(weather_dict)
6/8/23, 08:47 - Saurabh Bhau College: import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
import openpyxl

def submit_form():
    name = name_entry.get()
    father_name = father_name_entry.get()
    gender = gender_var.get()
    aadhar_card = aadhar_var.get()
    pan_card = pan_var.get()
    driving_license = driving_license_var.get()

    # Create a new Excel workbook or load an existing one
    workbook = openpyxl.Workbook()
    sheet = workbook.active

    # Write the form data to the Excel sheet
    sheet.append(['Name', 'Father Name', 'Gender', 'Aadhar Card', 'Pan Card', 'Driving License'])
    sheet.append([name, father_name, gender, aadhar_card, pan_card, driving_license])

    # Save the Excel file
    workbook.save('admission_enquiry.xlsx')

    # Display a success message
    messagebox.showinfo('Success', 'Form submitted and data stored in admission_enquiry.xlsx')

# Create the Tkinter window
window = tk.Tk()
window.title('Admission Enquiry Form')

# Create labels and entry fields
name_label = tk.Label(window, text='Name:')
name_label.pack()
name_entry = tk.Entry(window)
name_entry.pack()

father_name_label = tk.Label(window, text='Father Name:')
father_name_label.pack()
father_name_entry = tk.Entry(window)
father_name_entry.pack()

gender_label = tk.Label(window, text='Gender:')
gender_label.pack()
gender_var = tk.StringVar()
gender_choices = ['Male', 'Female', 'Other']
gender_dropdown = tk.OptionMenu(window, gender_var, *gender_choices)
gender_dropdown.pack()

aadhar_var = tk.BooleanVar()
aadhar_check = tk.Checkbutton(window, text='Do you have Aadhar Card', variable=aadhar_var)
aadhar_check.pack()

pan_var = tk.BooleanVar()
pan_check = tk.Checkbutton(window, text='Do you have Pan Card', variable=pan_var)
pan_check.pack()

driving_license_var = tk.BooleanVar()
driving_license_check = tk.Checkbutton(window, text='Do you have Driving License', variable=driving_license_var)
driving_license_check.pack()

submit_button = tk.Button(window, text='Submit', command=submit_form)
submit_button.pack()

window.mainloop()
6/8/23, 08:47 - Saurabh Bhau College: import tkinter as tk

def do_something():
    print("Menu item clicked")

def do_another_thing():
    print("Sub-menu item clicked")

# Create the Tkinter window
window = tk.Tk()

# Create a menu bar
menu_bar = tk.Menu(window)

# Create a File menu
file_menu = tk.Menu(menu_bar, tearoff=0)
file_menu.add_command(label="Open", command=do_something)
file_menu.add_separator()
file_menu.add_command(label="Exit", command=window.quit)

# Create an Edit menu
edit_menu = tk.Menu(menu_bar, tearoff=0)
edit_menu.add_command(label="Cut", command=do_something)
edit_menu.add_command(label="Copy", command=do_something)
edit_menu.add_command(label="Paste", command=do_something)

# Create a Sub-menu
sub_menu = tk.Menu(edit_menu, tearoff=0)
sub_menu.add_command(label="Sub-item", command=do_another_thing)
edit_menu.add_cascade(label="Sub-menu", menu=sub_menu)

# Add the menus to the menu bar
menu_bar.add_cascade(label="File", menu=file_menu)
menu_bar.add_cascade(label="Edit", menu=edit_menu)

# Configure the window to use the menu bar
window.config(menu=menu_bar)

window.mainloop()



import tkinter as tk

def convert():
    input_value = float(entry.get())

    if unit_var.get() == 'Centimeters':
        output_value = input_value / 100
    elif unit_var.get() == 'Inches':
        output_value = input_value * 0.0254
    elif unit_var.get() == 'Feet':
        output_value = input_value * 0.3048
    elif unit_var.get() == 'Meters':
        output_value = input_value

    result_label.config(text=f"{output_value:.2f} Meters")

# Create the Tkinter window
window = tk.Tk()
window.title('Length Converter')

# Create labels and entry fields
entry = tk.Entry(window)
entry.pack()

unit_var = tk.StringVar()
unit_var.set('Centimeters')
unit_dropdown = tk.OptionMenu(window, unit_var, 'Centimeters', 'Inches', 'Feet', 'Meters')
unit_dropdown.pack()

convert_button = tk.Button(window, text='Convert', command=convert)
convert_button.pack()

result_label = tk.Label(window, text='')
result_label.pack()

window.mainloop()
6/8/23, 08:47 - Saurabh Bhau College: import pandas as pd

data1 = {'Admission_No': [101, 102, 103, 104],
         'Name': ['John', 'Alice', 'Bob', 'Emma'],
         'Branch': ['CSE', 'IT', 'ECE', 'Mech']}
df1 = pd.DataFrame(data1)

data2 = {'Admission_No': [101, 102, 104, 105],
         'Marks': [90, 95, 88, 92]}
df2 = pd.DataFrame(data2)

# Merge df1 and df2 based on the 'Name' column (inner merge)
inner_merge = pd.merge(df1, df2, on='Admission_No', how='inner')
print("Inner Merge:")
print(inner_merge)

# Merge df1 and df2 based on the 'Name' column (outer merge)
outer_merge = pd.merge(df1, df2, on='Admission_No', how='outer')
print("\nOuter Merge:")
print(outer_merge)

data1 = {'Admission_No': [101, 102, 103, 104],

expression = ""
def press(num):
	global expression
	expression = expression + str(num)
	equation.set(expression)

def equalpress():
	try:
		global expression
		total = str(eval(expression))
		equation.set(total)
		expression = ""
	except:
		equation.set(" error ")
		expression = ""

def clear():
	global expression
	expression = ""
	equation.set("")

import tkinter as tk

# Function to add a task
def add_task():
    task = entry_task.get()
    if task:
        list_tasks.insert(tk.END, task)
        entry_task.delete(0, tk.END)

# Function to mark a task as completed
def mark_task():
    selected_task = list_tasks.curselection()
    if selected_task:
        list_tasks.itemconfig(selected_task, fg="gray", font="Arial 10 italic")

# Function to remove a task
def remove_task():
    selected_task = list_tasks.curselection()
    if selected_task:
        list_tasks.delete(selected_task)

# Function to clear all tasks
def clear_all_tasks():
    list_tasks.delete(0, tk.END)

# Create the main window
window = tk.Tk()
window.title("To-Do List")

# Create task entry field
entry_task = tk.Entry(window, width=40)
entry_task.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=10, pady=10)

# Create "Add" button
add_button = tk.Button(window, text="Add", command=add_task)
add_button.grid(row=0, column=1, padx=5, pady=10)

# Create task list
list_tasks = tk.Listbox(window, width=50, height=10)
list_tasks.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=10, pady=10)

# Create "Mark" button
mark_button = tk.Button(window, text="Mark Completed", command=mark_task)
mark_button.grid(row=2, column=0, padx=5, pady=5)

# Create "Remove" button
remove_button = tk.Button(window, text="Remove Task", command=remove_task)
remove_button.grid(row=2, column=1, padx=5, pady=5)

# Create "Clear All" button
clear_all_button = tk.Button(window, text="Clear All", command=clear_all_tasks)
clear_all_button.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=5, pady=10)

# Start the main event loop
window.mainloop()
6/9/23, 15:17 - Abhishek College: print("Question-2")
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog
from PIL import Image, ImageTk
import os

class ImageViewer:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Image Viewer")
        
        self.current_image = None
        self.current_index = 0
        self.images = []
        
        self.create_widgets()
    
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Image display area
        self.image_label = tk.Label(self.root)
        self.image_label.pack(padx=10, pady=10)
        
        # Navigation buttons
        nav_frame = tk.Frame(self.root)
        nav_frame.pack(pady=5)
        
        prev_button = tk.Button(nav_frame, text="Previous", command=self.show_previous_image)
        prev_button.pack(side=tk.LEFT)
        
        next_button = tk.Button(nav_frame, text="Next", command=self.show_next_image)
        next_button.pack(side=tk.LEFT)
        
        # File browser button
        browse_button = tk.Button(self.root, text="Browse", command=self.browse_images)
        browse_button.pack(pady=5)
        
    def browse_images(self):
        filetypes = (("Image files", ("*.jpg", "*.jpeg", "*.png", "*.gif", "*.bmp")), ("All files", "*.*"))
        selected_files = filedialog.askopenfilenames(filetypes=filetypes)
        
        if selected_files:
            self.images = list(selected_files)
            self.current_index = 0
            self.show_image()
        
    def show_image(self):
        if self.images:
            image_path = self.images[self.current_index]
            image = Image.open(image_path)
            
            # Scale the image to fit within the available space without distorting its aspect ratio
            width, height = image.size
            max_width = self.root.winfo_width() - 20
            max_height = self.root.winfo_height() - 70
            
            if width > max_width or height > max_height:
                ratio = min(max_width / width, max_height / height)
                new_width = int(width * ratio)
                new_height = int(height * ratio)
                image = image.resize((new_width, new_height), Image.ANTIALIAS)
            
            # Update the image label
            self.current_image = ImageTk.PhotoImage(image)
            self.image_label.config(image=self.current_image)
    
    def show_previous_image(self):
        if self.current_index > 0:
            self.current_index -= 1
            self.show_image()
    
    def show_next_image(self):
        if self.current_index < len(self.images) - 1:
            self.current_index += 1
            self.show_image()

root = tk.Tk()
app = ImageViewer(root)
root.mainloop()
6/9/23, 15:18 - Abhishek College: print("Question-3")
import tkinter as tk
def convert_temperature():
    try:
        temperature = float(entry_temperature.get())

        input_unit =input_unit_var.get()
        output_unit = output_unit_var.get()

        if input_unit == output_unit:
            converted_temp = temperature
        elif input_unit == "Celsius" and output_unit == "Fahrenheit":
            converted_temp = temperature * 9/5 + 32
        elif input_unit == "Celsius" and output_unit == "Kelvin":
            converted_temp = temperature + 273.15
        elif input_unit == "Fahrenheit" and output_unit == "Celsius":
            converted_temp = (temperature - 32) * 5/9
        elif input_unit == "Fahrenheit" and output_unit == "Kelvin":
            converted_temp = (temperature - 32) * 5/9 + 273.15
        elif input_unit == "Kelvin" and output_unit == "Celsius":
            converted_temp = temperature - 273.15
        elif input_unit == "Kelvin" and output_unit == "Fahrenheit":
            converted_temp = (temperature - 273.15) * 9/5 + 32

        result_label.config(text=str(round(converted_temp, 2)))
    except ValueError:
        result_label.config(text="Invalid input")

# Create the main window
window = tk.Tk()
window.title("Temperature Converter")

# Create temperature input field
entry_temperature = tk.Entry(window)
entry_temperature.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=10, pady=10)

# Create input unit dropdown menu
input_unit_var = tk.StringVar(window)
input_unit_var.set("Celsius")
input_unit_dropdown = tk.OptionMenu(window, input_unit_var, "Celsius", "Fahrenheit", "Kelvin")
input_unit_dropdown.grid(row=0, column=1, padx=10, pady=10)

# Create output unit dropdown menu
output_unit_var = tk.StringVar(window)
output_unit_var.set("Fahrenheit")
output_unit_dropdown = tk.OptionMenu(window, output_unit_var, "Celsius", "Fahrenheit", "Kelvin")
output_unit_dropdown.grid(row=0, column=2, padx=10, pady=10)

# Create conversion button
convert_button = tk.Button(window, text="Convert", command=convert_temperature)
convert_button.grid(row=0, column=3, padx=10, pady=10)

# Create result label
result_label = tk.Label(window, text="")
result_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=4, padx=10, pady=10)

# Start the main event loop
window.mainloop()
6/9/23, 15:18 - Abhishek College: print("Question-4")
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import numpy as np

def calculate_population(t):
    e = 2.718
    population = (15000 * (1 + t)) / (15 + e)
    return population

# Specify the time interval
start_time = 0
end_time = 10
step = 0.1

# Create an array of time values
time = np.arange(start_time, end_time, step)

# Calculate the population at each time point
population = calculate_population(time)
print("Population at different times is:",population)

# Plot the graph
plt.plot(time, population)
plt.xlabel('Time (hours)')
plt.ylabel('Population')
plt.title('Bacterial Population Growth')
plt.grid(True)
plt.show()

import numpy as np

# Define the matrices
A = np.array([[1, 0], [0, 1]])
B = np.array([[1, 2], [3, 4]])

# 1. Inverse of each matrix
A_inverse = np.linalg.inv(A)
B_inverse = np.linalg.inv(B)
print("Inverse of matrix A:")
print(A_inverse)
print("\nInverse of matrix B:")
print(B_inverse)

# 2. Addition and subtraction
addition_result = A + B
subtraction_result = A - B
print("\nAddition of matrices A and B:")
print(addition_result)
print("\nSubtraction of matrix B from matrix A:")
print(subtraction_result)

# 3. Multiplication
multiplication_result = np.matmul(A, B)
print("\nMultiplication of matrices A and B:")
print(multiplication_result)

public class Main {
    public static void main(String[] args) {

        int seconds = sc.nextInt();

10/6/23, 14:33 - Saurabh Bhau College: def quick_sort(arr):
    if len(arr) <= 1:
        return arr
    else:
        pivot = arr[0]
        left = []
        right = []
        equal = []
        for x in arr:
            if x < pivot:
                left.append(x)
            elif x > pivot:
                right.append(x)
            else:
                equal.append(x)
        return quick_sort(left) + equal + quick_sort(right)

# Example usage
unsorted_array = [7, 2, 1, 6, 8, 5, 3, 4, 7]
sorted_array = quick_sort(unsorted_array)
print("Sorted Array:", sorted_array)

10/25/23, 20:17 - ğ•¬ğ–“ğ–ğ–ğ–™ College: Greetings from AICTE !

As you are already aware that Yuva Sangam is Yuva Sangam is a flagship program of the Ek Bharat Shreshtha Bharat (EBSB) initiative, launched by the Hon'ble Prime Minister of India. This initiative focuses on conducting exposure tours of the youths comprising mainly students studying in Higher Educational institutions (HEIs) & some off-campus youths from one state to other states & vice versa. It provides an immersive experience of various facets of life, development landmarks, recent achievements and a youth connect in the host state. The program aims to promote national integration and understanding by connecting youth from different parts of the country through educational and cultural exchanges.

In addition to the cultural exchange, Yuva Sangam also includes a number of other activities that are designed to help students develop their leadership, sports and soft skills. For example, students may get an opportunity not only to participate in workshops on leadership, communication, and teamwork but also sports events that may be organised by SAI. They will also have the opportunity to meet and interact with VVIPs, celebrities or important personalities of the host state.

The success of Yuva Sangam Phase 1 and 2 is a testament to the importance of investing in youth and building bridges between different communities. The program has had a positive impact on the lives of thousands of youth and has helped to build a more united and inclusive India.

I request your support in motivating students of your institution to register for Yuva Sangam Phase-3, a student exchange program under EBSB.

All interested students can register online at https://ebsb.aicte-india.org/

The registration process has started on 18-10-2023 and the last date is 28-10-2023.
